<div id="review_1637838237" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1637838237" />
    <a title="Jodi Perkins" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/35630963-jodi-perkins"><img alt="Jodi Perkins" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1446605149p2/35630963.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1637838237?book_show_action=true">May 14, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jodi Perkins" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jodi Perkins" href="/user/show/35630963-jodi-perkins">Jodi Perkins</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35630963-jodi-perkins?shelf=adult-fiction">adult-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35630963-jodi-perkins?shelf=literary-fiction">literary-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35630963-jodi-perkins?shelf=philosophical">philosophical</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35630963-jodi-perkins?shelf=humor">humor</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35630963-jodi-perkins?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35630963-jodi-perkins?shelf=cultural">cultural</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35630963-jodi-perkins?shelf=satire">satire</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35630963-jodi-perkins?shelf=indian">indian</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35630963-jodi-perkins?shelf=indian-literature">indian-literature</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35630963-jodi-perkins?shelf=asian-american">asian-american</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1637838237" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9142232226318092006"><i>Coinman: An Untold Conspiracy</i> is a literary fiction that takes everyday workplace dynamics to preposterous levels in a satirical story written with much intelligence and dry wit. <br/><br/>What I loved most about this quirky little tale is that anyone with a job can relate to Coinman’s plight. On the one hand, much of the bullying behaviors performed by the sadistic antagonist Hukum (and the rest of the staff) seems to be an unrealistic stretch for adults, and is more reminiscent of playground behavior th</span>
  <span id="freeText9142232226318092006" style="display:none"><i>Coinman: An Untold Conspiracy</i> is a literary fiction that takes everyday workplace dynamics to preposterous levels in a satirical story written with much intelligence and dry wit. <br /><br />What I loved most about this quirky little tale is that anyone with a job can relate to Coinman’s plight. On the one hand, much of the bullying behaviors performed by the sadistic antagonist Hukum (and the rest of the staff) seems to be an unrealistic stretch for adults, and is more reminiscent of playground behavior than that which transpires in an office. On the other hand, I found this exaggeration of behaviors to be not only entertaining, but also an effective literary device--one used as a deliberate social commentary on the nature of cattiness and gossip-mongering in the workplace. Even though I, the reader, have never been humiliated by a malicious and vile poem posted in the workroom, or any of the other absurd bullying tactics that Coinman suffers, at the minimum I can connect with that feeling of being left out of a clique, or talked about. <br /><br />In many ways, <i>Coinman: An Untold Conspiracy</i> reminds me of a caricature, managing to capture and explore the human condition by garish means. Is it absurdly exaggerated? Yes. But this exaggeration is deliberate and intended to highlight real truths. I could easily see this novel being incorporated as required reading in a college course exploring social aspects of human behavior.<br /><br />Thank you to author Pawan Mishra, who contacted me to give an honest and unbiased review.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="9142232226318092006" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1651242461" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1651242461" />
    <a title="Damian Maher" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/48258938-damian-maher"><img alt="Damian Maher" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_50x66-632230dc9882b4352d753eedf9396530.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1651242461?book_show_action=true">May 28, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Damian Maher" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Damian Maher" href="/user/show/48258938-damian-maher">Damian Maher</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/48258938-damian-maher?shelf=humor">humor</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/48258938-damian-maher?shelf=satire">satire</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/48258938-damian-maher?shelf=indian">indian</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/48258938-damian-maher?shelf=fiction">fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/48258938-damian-maher?shelf=comedy">comedy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1651242461" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8692504055784678672">This was a great read! It explores an eccentric workers habit of jiggling coins, which leads him to be subjected to bullying by the coworkers. Trying not to reveal too much about the story or the plot, let me explain why I love this book so much.<br/><br/>Most importantly, I find the writing to be honest and passionate. The satirical aspect is brought with intelligence and wit; exaggerations are intended to highlight the universal truths of life. <br/><br/>Mishra has vividly written the characters into existence; t</span>
  <span id="freeText8692504055784678672" style="display:none">This was a great read! It explores an eccentric workers habit of jiggling coins, which leads him to be subjected to bullying by the coworkers. Trying not to reveal too much about the story or the plot, let me explain why I love this book so much.<br /><br />Most importantly, I find the writing to be honest and passionate. The satirical aspect is brought with intelligence and wit; exaggerations are intended to highlight the universal truths of life. <br /><br />Mishra has vividly written the characters into existence; the psychodynamics of main characters are well thought through and masterfully described. This depth adds another dimension to the comic aspect; it is never cheap or shallow. I laughed many times, but I’ve also learned about many aspects of social interactions. <br /><br />The plot grabbed my attention; on many occasions I eagerly awaited what will happen. The story is told very well and it took me often into the unsuspected directions. There are many interesting anecdotes depicting the Indian culture, but they also very relatable to readers in other cultures. <br /><br />This book is original, unique and odd…in the most magical way. It is certainly not from the department “more of the same”. Read it if you are looking for something fresh, juicy and different! I will most certainly reread this book from time to time, because it is hard to leave the world the author has created. I am looking forward to reading the next Mishra’s book!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="8692504055784678672" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1546483451" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1546483451" />
    <a title="Saleh Radaideh" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15997912-saleh-radaideh"><img alt="Saleh Radaideh" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1490840919p2/15997912.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1546483451?book_show_action=true">Feb 12, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Saleh Radaideh" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Saleh Radaideh" href="/user/show/15997912-saleh-radaideh">Saleh Radaideh</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1546483451" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9870081173915098733">This is a very interesting read. I found it hilarious and entertaining. Coinman is such a funny, laughable character who I would want to be friends with. There are many incidents throughout the story and in the office where one would laugh hysterically. Caught between the stress at home with his wife, Imli, an actress, and his goofy friends at work, Coinman goes on all sorts of crazy, humorous stunts in order to cope with these people. It turns out that Coinman isn't even his real name! His sill</span>
  <span id="freeText9870081173915098733" style="display:none">This is a very interesting read. I found it hilarious and entertaining. Coinman is such a funny, laughable character who I would want to be friends with. There are many incidents throughout the story and in the office where one would laugh hysterically. Caught between the stress at home with his wife, Imli, an actress, and his goofy friends at work, Coinman goes on all sorts of crazy, humorous stunts in order to cope with these people. It turns out that Coinman isn't even his real name! His silly friends at the office renamed him from Kesar to Coinman due to Coinman's deep appreciation for the coin. The gossip from the office about this nickname ended up consuming his whole life and every thing with his real name on it. There's a lot of background to the humor, which makes the humor even better. I think that this book is unique when it comes to its humor, as I don't come across many books as funny as this one. This is a very entertaining story, and I recommend it to anyone looking for a fun read, and something interesting and unique.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9870081173915098733" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1633968594" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1633968594" />
    <a title="Katja Vartiainen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/43112027-katja-vartiainen"><img alt="Katja Vartiainen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1601391634p2/43112027.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1633968594?book_show_action=true">May 10, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katja Vartiainen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katja Vartiainen" href="/user/show/43112027-katja-vartiainen">Katja Vartiainen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/27504365-coinman">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43112027-katja-vartiainen?shelf=satire">satire</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43112027-katja-vartiainen?shelf=humour">humour</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43112027-katja-vartiainen?shelf=fiction">fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43112027-katja-vartiainen?shelf=indian">indian</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1633968594" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1101875004046709615">This is an enjoyable novel about a man with a peculiar habit and events in his life. I have never lived the office life, and it seems to be a reproduction of the school class, as in this story. The author, Pawan Mishra, describes well the tyranny of the bullies and the group dynamics. This is why I call this a novel, not so much as humor. It made me more pensive than it made me giggle. Which is not a bad thing. There are a lot of interesting, bizarre characters and twists in the story. All comed</span>
  <span id="freeText1101875004046709615" style="display:none">This is an enjoyable novel about a man with a peculiar habit and events in his life. I have never lived the office life, and it seems to be a reproduction of the school class, as in this story. The author, Pawan Mishra, describes well the tyranny of the bullies and the group dynamics. This is why I call this a novel, not so much as humor. It made me more pensive than it made me giggle. Which is not a bad thing. There are a lot of interesting, bizarre characters and twists in the story. All comedy balances on the razor's edge. On the other side is laughter, on the other awaits tragedy. Both are hysterical, and most of the great comedians have been depressive. It is a tough job to find the light int he tragedy and convey it to others. This made me think about my own mprojects and definitions... ANYWAY. The author likes to juggle with dialogue, which is quite amusing. The end seemed a bit rushed. We'll wait for the next one.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1101875004046709615" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1636549733" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13044725107899528850">“The mind numbing sound of relentlessly jingling coins was something the people of the office, the center stage of this story, hadn’t quite learned to live with yet…”<br/><br/>Coinman is an absolute delight! I found myself absorbed in the life of this low level office worker in Northern India. His eccentricities are intriguing and I found myself laughing out loud in amusement at some of the antics that happen in his life. His wife and boss are a trip to read and you find yourself rooting for this man to o</span>
  <span id="freeText13044725107899528850" style="display:none">“The mind numbing sound of relentlessly jingling coins was something the people of the office, the center stage of this story, hadn’t quite learned to live with yet…”<br /><br />Coinman is an absolute delight! I found myself absorbed in the life of this low level office worker in Northern India. His eccentricities are intriguing and I found myself laughing out loud in amusement at some of the antics that happen in his life. His wife and boss are a trip to read and you find yourself rooting for this man to overcome his obstacles. The conspiracy held against Kelsar, aka Coinman, by his co-workers, and their interactions, are what keep this story interesting. Although humorous, the story also pulls at your heartstrings. A refreshingly great story!<br /></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('peqlJYmBeF0IJCc67jCVvdBjGjeX1Ebsx6tbefcdUhflmlj+dhETL13ZvMl943HYIHUJ/FTpTuZtwIETFneWyA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('V71L4is2WsAZYq21cL7/XsQeeKJUH6pFRn8ysLI9ISMXzbY51KYxskyfNkbjbRs7NAhraZciok/sFOjaU1fl/A==')})
  }

      <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/14594440.Pawan_Mishra">About Pawan Mishra</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/14594440.Pawan_Mishra"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1476500668p3/14594440.jpg);'></div>
</a></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__widgetContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__name'>
<a href="/author/show/14594440.Pawan_Mishra">Pawan Mishra
</a></div>
<div class='goodreadsAuthorBadge'></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__followerCount'>
180
followers
</div>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer4705991917126887544">Born in 1976 in Aligarh, India, Pawan Mishra is an award-winning author, producer, director, and a leader in finance and technology industries. In Jan 2017 Huffington Post listed his novel "Coinman: An Untold Conspiracy" as one of the best independently published fiction books of year 2016. He conceptualized, produced, and directed the animation series "My Teacher Hilda".<br/><br/>He completed his education</span>
  <span id="freeText4705991917126887544" style="display:none">Born in 1976 in Aligarh, India, Pawan Mishra is an award-winning author, producer, director, and a leader in finance and technology industries. In Jan 2017 Huffington Post listed his novel "Coinman: An Untold Conspiracy" as one of the best independently published fiction books of year 2016. He conceptualized, produced, and directed the animation series "My Teacher Hilda".<br /><br />He completed his education at the Indian Institute of Technology, Kanpur. Pawan lives in Apex, North Carolina, with his wife, Ritu, and two daughters, Mitali and Myra.<br /><br />Visit him at: <br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.pawanmishra.com">www.pawanmishra.com</a><br />pawanmishrablogs.wordpress.com<br /><br />"The richness of the world around us constantly inspires me to write in a way that's humorous and symbolic at the same time. The small spontaneous things that constitute this beauty, sometimes bright and dark at other times, have so much left unsaid still that I find myself up against an immense number of doors. Coinman was one of such doors which opened several others as soon as I knocked on it." ~Pawan Mishra</span>
  <a data-text-id="4705991917126887544" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>
</div>

a call to SignInPromptController#get to determine if the user should see the sign in interstial.

last seen the insterstitial.  If the controller responds indicating the popup should appear, the
React component will render its content.
-->
